  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d6660be0-1a94-424c-8010-668c1bb58ee6'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

  <span id="freeText5101889515628057991" style="display:none"><i>Book 2 in the New Species series. The books can be read as stand-alone stories, but it is advisable to read them in order to get the most enjoyment from the series.</i><br /><br />Dr. Trisha Norbit is flat on her back in a hospital bed, pinned under a really big New Species male. Though drugged out of his mind, he promises her ecstasy and is determined to deliver—but hospital staff intervenes. 215 is a man Trisha will never forget. But, when she meets him again at Homeland…he doesn’t even remember her!<br /><br />The nosy new doctor wants to know all about the breeding habits between humans and Species. Slade proposes a hands-on education but she’s not interested in a one-night stand. He can’t offer more because he’s haunted by the memory of a woman he once tried to claim. He’s shocked when he realizes they are one and the same. He’s blown it—she’ll never give him a chance now.<br /><br />But, when her life is in danger, he’s the only one who can save her. As they flee through the wilderness, their desire ignites and cannot be denied. Hot sex, on the run, has consequences that are even more dangerous and will change their lives forever.<br /><br />Reader Advisory: There is a scene of an attempted rape.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1206227172" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7170176715238872898"><b> 3.5 Wishy Washy stars</b><br/><br/><b>*Spoilers*</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/797209_zpsmwu1ysyy.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424709576ra/13794101.gif' alt=' photo 797209_zpsmwu1ysyy.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Slade snorted. “Women.” “Men.” “Smartass.” “Dumbass.”</b><br/><br/><br/>When I read a shifter book I expect a fated soul mate kind of love. That bam! your are mine and I knew it the minute we met kinda thing. The I am never going to let you go thing . I got that kind of love in the first book with Fury and was looking forward to some more in this book, but what I got was Slade!<br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/giphy%205_zpscwn2jwjx.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424709576ra/13794102.gif' alt=' photo giphy 5_zpscwn2jwjx.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>“You’re mine, Doc. I’d fight anyone to get you back and I’ll kill any man who touches you.”</b><br/><br/><br/>Slade:<br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/download%204_zpsbfm0os2h.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
 </a></span>
  <span id="freeText7170176715238872898" style="display:none"><b> 3.5 Wishy Washy stars</b><br><br><b>*Spoilers*</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/797209_zpsmwu1ysyy.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>Slade snorted. “Women.” “Men.” “Smartass.” “Dumbass.”</b><br><br><br>When I read a shifter book I expect a fated soul mate kind of love. That bam! your are mine and I knew it the minute we met kinda thing. The I am never going to let you go thing . I got that kind of love in the first book with Fury and was looking forward to some more in this book, but what I got was Slade!<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/giphy%205_zpscwn2jwjx.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I didn't like Slade . He annoyed the shit outta me! he was wishy washy, jerky and kind of a chicken in this book . I thought he would get better in the book, but by the time he comes around I already didn't like him and he didn't do anything redeeming to make me soften to him. I didn't hate him he wasn't such a asshole that I couldn't stand him or anything , he was kinda like the little boy in 3rd grade that pulls your hair and flings mud at you because he likes you, and he never grows up! Then at towards the end he just sees the light and loves her, is never letting her go and all is good. I don't think so! He also called her sweet thing all the time making me picture him in my head like this<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/leon-phelps_zpsxw1dojxg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>This is my impersonation of Slade. <br>"I love you and I will be with you forever and I will fight anyone to keep you safe and get you back your mine!" " Sike!!!! Ha I was just jokin I'm out bitch see ya. " " Okay wait a minute I think I do want you after all. Yes , yes I do! Your mine again!!!"<br><br><br><b>“Bend over for me, Trisha. I’m going to fuck you the way I’ve wanted to since I saw you. I’m going to drive so deep into that wet little sheath of yours until you don’t know where I end and you begin. I bet you’re going to be so tight that you fist around my dick and I have to fight to move inside you.”<br><br><br>“I missed you,” he breathed against her skin. “I won’t ever leave you again. Ever, Trisha. I’d rather die than be away from you. I swear to protect you with my life and I won’t mess up again. I learned how much you mean to me.”</b><br><br>Trisha:<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/861f1c83fe60800f9e4ab353d43dc65811_zpspkljx9d9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>“Make me forget. Please? I want you.”</b><br><br>Damn I loved Trisha, she totally made this book for me! She made up for what Slade lacked and she is the reason the book got 3.5 stars instead of 2! She was Brave, smart and Sassy. She fought for what she believed in and even in the face of death and rape she was brave and strong. I love that she didn't hold back and just told you what she thought! I don't think I would change a thing about her!<br><br><b>“I’d rather die. Just kill me!” she screamed at him. “You’re a fucking loser. You’re nothing but a fucking asshole rapest.” She hoped he’d snap and kill her. She’d rather die than live through him touching her. “And that’s fucking pathetic by the way. I’m a doctor and I’ve seen a lot of them,” she taunted him. “Pathetic!” she screamed.<br><br><br><br>“You mean ‘bastard’, don’t you? Go to hell, Slade. Yes, the baby is yours in the biological way. In every other sense the baby is mine and mine alone. Don’t worry though. In the last weeks I’ve learned exactly what to expect from you so stay away from me just the way you have been. I waited a week for you to call or come see me. When you didn’t I was even hopeful for another week. Then you took this job and didn’t even have the decency to tell me you were leaving. You just left. I hate you for that, I really do, and I will never forgive you. You lied to me and you just blew me off. Well, I can do that too. Leave me alone and stop beating up my friends, because they actually care about me.” She took a ragged breath, fighting the urge to cry. “They don’t make me cry. They don’t abandon me or break my heart.” </b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/10410896_1557776124492019_8854553213671600625_n11_zpsktacwh47.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424709576i/13794106._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 10410896_1557776124492019_8854553213671600625_n11_zpsktacwh47.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>“I love being inside you.” Trisha turned her head against his chest. “I love you being there. Wow, Slade. Just wow.”</b><br><br><br>Even with Slade being a immature asshat for a good part of the book. It was still a pretty good read. There wasn't enough romance, but the sex was hott, and the friendships between Trisha, Brass, Moon, and Harley was too cute, and of course there is the baby. I am a sucker for babies!!!!!<br><br>Here is my favorite moment in the book:<br><br><b>“Oh God,” she moaned.<br>His mouth withdrew from her sensitive flesh. “I told you I was going to kiss you.”<br>“I thought you’d aim for my mouth.”<br>He tilted his head, regarding her. “Do you want me to stop? I have to admit I don’t want to. I’ve been dying to taste every inch of you. Don’t deny me, sweet thing.”<br>“Do you want to die? That’s what will happen if you do stop. Please continue.”</b><br><br><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsession.blogspot.com/">http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsessio...</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer890365870" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5002194192659384320">As I mentioned in my review of the 1st book in the series <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12063467-fury?ac=1'>https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1...</a> , I was a bit apprehensive continuing reading the next book. Fury reminded me a lot of Lora Leigh's Breed Series, but I decided to read the next story and I was, despite the similarities, quite impressed.<br/><br/>I did enjoy Slade's story more than Fury. <br/>Slade is part human/canine...gorgeous, naturally..<img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395670067i/9026872.jpg' alt=' photo 44db0bde3059eb37221d98afbcecc4be_zps15eb4184.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>He falls in love with Trisha Norbitt, the Homeland (home of the new species)doctor. Soon they embark on a</span>
  <span id="freeText5002194192659384320" style="display:none">As I mentioned in my review of the 1st book in the series <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12063467-fury?ac=1">https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1...</a> , I was a bit apprehensive continuing reading the next book. Fury reminded me a lot of Lora Leigh's Breed Series, but I decided to read the next story and I was, despite the similarities, quite impressed.<br><br>I did enjoy Slade's story more than Fury. <br>Slade is part human/canine...gorgeous, naturally..<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395670067i/9026872.jpg" alt=" photo 44db0bde3059eb37221d98afbcecc4be_zps15eb4184.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He falls in love with Trisha Norbitt, the Homeland (home of the new species)doctor. Soon they embark on a steamy and sizzling relationship <blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395670067ra/9026873.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mwpsjmspF31rp3ejzo6_400_zps95607e12.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote> - they do a lot of this....geez, these new species guys are totally sexed!!! And of course, totally protective and domineering...<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395670067i/9026874.jpg" alt=" photo download2_zpsaf515b4b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>We get to know more about the New Species and the atrocities committed to them, we meet new characters and we get to know more about the ones we met previously and I am kind of getting "lured" into their world.<br><br>Loved the banter between Slade &amp; Trisha and between her and the guys guarding her...some hilarious moments and some of the things Smiley &amp; the gang said and did....funny and cute...how they learn new sayings and more about us humans!!<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395670067i/9026875.jpg" alt="Slade by Laurann Dohner photo download_zpsfedd3b88.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br><br>I think I am going to like this series..onto book #3 next!!!</span>

    <a title="Alp" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26653561-alp"><img alt="Alp" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1462791280p2/26653561.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1508947354?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alp" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alp" href="/user/show/26653561-alp">Alp</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26653561-alp?shelf=sci-fi-romance">sci-fi-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26653561-alp?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26653561-alp?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1508947354" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11634197876171912919">Not what I expected… It wasn't bad but wasn't amazing either. The first half of the book was so boring that I almost DNF'd. Slade and Trisha kept running away and hiding from the bad guys who came to hunt them down in the woods. They were in the woods half the book! And there was almost no story here! Slade had repeatedly ticked me off when he kept giving her hot and cold treatment. I don't understand what was wrong with him that he kept calling her Doc. Yes, she's a doctor but she has her name,</span>
  <span id="freeText11634197876171912919" style="display:none">Not what I expected… It wasn't bad but wasn't amazing either. The first half of the book was so boring that I almost DNF'd. Slade and Trisha kept running away and hiding from the bad guys who came to hunt them down in the woods. They were in the woods half the book! And there was almost no story here! Slade had repeatedly ticked me off when he kept giving her hot and cold treatment. I don't understand what was wrong with him that he kept calling her Doc. Yes, she's a doctor but she has her name, and her name is Trisha. Jerk!<br /><br />The second half was much better. There was drama about Trisha’s pregnancy that helped pull me out of my bad mood. Thankfully, Slade could redeem himself in the last quarter of the book, otherwise you might see me ranting on about him much more than this!<br /><br />And about the heroine, Trisha, there was not much depth to her character. I knew she’s a doctor, graduated from medical school at a very young age, and that’s it. There was no mention of her personality or background so I felt like I couldn’t connect with her (as a character).<br /><br />I found the story was overly long and the sex scenes weren’t appealing enough to hold my attention. I skimmed through some of them just to finish the book. The best thing about this book is Brass. He is very funny and caring. He really should be a hero!<br /><br />However, I liked the second half and it was nice enough to make me want to continue this series. And that was the reason why I gave it 3 stars.<br /><br /><br />**BR with my lovely friend, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4150124-aileene" rel="nofollow noopener">Aileene</a>.</span>

They meet at the hospital, right after the New Species are freed from Mercile industries. An intimate meeting experienced like no other, stays with the two long after their separation. Seeking a way to learn more on New Species, Trisha applies and accepts a job at Homeland, where New Species currently live. With the memory</span>
  <span id="freeText6075606010653097750" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>He would have gone days without food or water just to know her body.</b>
</i><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382784791i/6196954._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Slade, the second book in the New Species series, features Dr Trisha Norbit and Slade, an NSO officer. They meet at the hospital, right after the New Species are freed from Mercile industries. An intimate meeting experienced like no other, stays with the two long after their separation. Seeking a way to learn more on New Species, Trisha applies and accepts a job at Homeland, where New Species currently live. With the memory of her encounter with Slade always haunting her, Trisha is surprised and disappointed to find Slade doesn't remember her from the hospital.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382784693i/6196837._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Slade</b> previously known as 215, can't forget the sexy redhead he woke up to at the hospital. She haunts him on a nightly basis with thoughts of their encounter and fantasies of finding her again. He makes a fool of himself by acting like an ass towards Trisha with his crude come-ons and rude comments. Seeking a way to redeem himself, Slade works to seduce Trisha and to retrain his intense need for her by giving her what she deserves. Only not all plans are followed through when planed by a horny New Species male, with the female of his dreams ready for the taking. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382784935i/6197016._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These two are intimate in the least expected places and at the most inconvenient times. But...its still sexy as hell. Especially all the dirty talk growled by Slade *sigh*<br><br><i>
  <b>"Bend over for me, Trisha. I'm going to fuck you the way I've wanted to since I saw you." </b>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382785106ra/6197162.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm usually all for a romantic setting, on a bed cuddling, but with these New Species males and their love for <b>'mounting'</b>, mate I've found my new preference there. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382785106i/6197164._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382790213ra/6200541.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Trisha</b>, a doctor at Homeland, wanted Slade from the moment he touched her. A trip out of Homeland brings Trisha and Slade to great danger, with the two fighting for survival. Dependent on Slade, Trisha forms a close bond with her protector. But will all be the same between them after they return to Homeland? Will her feelings be shared by Slade, or will all be forgotten? Well, go read it to find out people!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382785106i/6197163._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Suspenseful, heart stopping read, that's full of surprises that <b>shocked</b> and pleased me extremely. But even saying that, I will admit to loving <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12063467.Fury__New_Species___1_" title="Fury (New Species, #1) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Fury</a>, book one in this series more. It just didn't hit the "OMG I love this book" mark for me. From the relationship formed, to Slade's thick-headedness, at times I was left a tad disappointed. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382784935i/6197017._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I will definatly be continuing this fantastic series and recommend it HIGHLY to all my PNR lover mates, who love a bit of animal in their men xx<br><br><u>My New Species Reviews:</u><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/717777857" rel="nofollow noopener">Fury (New Species #1) </a></b></span>

<div id="review_1570945805" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1570945805" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1570945805?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1570945805" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1184189748265731239">Comparing this book to the first one is like comparing carob to chocolate. Sure, carob looks and smells like chocolate, but it doesn't taste even half as good.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457299965i/18344394._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>That is a cruel trick, mom!<br/><br/>The New Species world is really cool. We have these science experiment people who are half animal/half human trying to simply exist. They aren't trying to mess with the humans, interact with them much, take their jobs, or hurt anyone. They have their own compounds to live in even. So, what's the problem?<br/><br/>The probl</span>
  <span id="freeText1184189748265731239" style="display:none">Comparing this book to the first one is like comparing carob to chocolate. Sure, carob looks and smells like chocolate, but it doesn't taste even half as good.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457299965i/18344394._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>That is a cruel trick, mom!<br><br>The New Species world is really cool. We have these science experiment people who are half animal/half human trying to simply exist. They aren't trying to mess with the humans, interact with them much, take their jobs, or hurt anyone. They have their own compounds to live in even. So, what's the problem?<br><br>The problem is that anything new and different = fear.<br>Fear = anger<br>Anger = kill them all!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457299965i/18344395.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As far as the back-woods dumbass hillybilly hunter boys are concerned, it's open season on New Species. They want to get them some of those there animal heads to mount on their walls. Cuz, there's nothing classier than a room full of animal corpses.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457299965i/18344396.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, in the last book we met Trisha, the human doctor for the New Species, and Slade, one of the New Species police officers. She was very smart and cool, and he was a little bit of a jerk. So, it shouldn't have surprised me that he was a much bigger jerk in this book. And, he was! He jerked it up, baby!!<br><br>They are traveling together to a location that the leader is looking at to buy more land for their people. But, word gets through to a hate group and they are run off the road in the mountains and then it's redneck hunting time! Git yur guns, boys! So, Trisha and Slade are running through the woods, trying to not get killed.<br><br>So, being the gentleman that he is, Slade informs Trisha that she can lay close to him that night to stay warm only if she gives him a handy. Really? That's our hero?<br><br><b>
  <i>"Want to keep warm, Doc?.... either rub me or move away."<br><br>"Release my hand."<br><br>He didn't. He moved it against him.</i>
</b><br><br>I don't know about you, but I think this is pretty rapey behavior. He pulled that crap on me and I'd put his balls in a vice grip until he cried like a girl. But, of course, she ends up having sex with him in the dirt. After running for their lives and peeing in the woods all day without food or water. Romantic!<br><br>That was my problem with the book. Slade was all "I love her, I'd do anything for her" in his thoughts, but he was rude, crude, and abusive in his language towards her. I just couldn't like this guy. He is on my I-wish-I-could-kill-this-book-character list. I'm tempted to join one of the hate groups that is trying to hunt him. I can buy some camo. I can learn to spit and scratch myself.<br><br>There are good parts of this book, too, though. Trisha has three guards that have become her best buddies and they are fun and hilarious. Harley was my favorite. He was constantly cracking jokes. <br><br><b>
  <i>"A friend? I thought we could elope to Vegas and have Elvis marry us."<br>...He lifted up the material on his arm. "I had a spot picked out here to have your name tattooed on me and I thought I could have my name tattooed across your ass. That way I could actually say I owned your ass."</i>
</b><br><br>The other two guys, Brass and Moon were also really funny. They provided the personality that I wish Slade had.<br><br>Oh well. On to the next book, but I'm nervous because the guy it's about was a huge alpha in this one. Maybe he'll be nice and sweet in the next one..... it's possible...<br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1184189748265731239" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

I'M WORTH IT. </b><br><br><br>He gave it to me, alright, but I was nowhere near impressed.<br><br>To start off, this is the second installment of New Species where it has showcased Slade and the nosy Doctor "Doc" Trisha Norbit.<br><br>Their first encounter was a sizzle and it got me REALLY excited, however as I continued on, my excitement and focus wavered.<br><br><i>So did I like their story?</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453292761ra/17807728.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am a big fan of teasing and Slade was a big tease. But I HATED IT! I detested him. He was crude and a jackass. <br>The words that came out of his mouth were just wrong. <br>I imagined his mouth sewn shut like this <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453292761ra/17807729.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I'll be like<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453292761ra/17807730.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But of course that didn't happen in the story.<br><b> *TSK!* </b><br><br><i>So, the story grabbed me then?</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453292761i/17807731.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>On two occasions only.<br>1. Slade and Trisha's survival scenes. The action was great and the author injected small doses of violence. Both have satisfied me right to my core.<br>2. Valiant. This big hunk floats my boat. I WANT TO GET TO KNOW HIM. I WANT TO KNOW WHAT TICKLE HIS PICKLE.<br><br><i>So, would I give this a higher rating?</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453292761i/17807732.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>(Coz) Apart from Slade being an asshat and his untimely innuendos, banter between the New Species and Trisha didn't sit well with me. It was annoyingly silly (ESP poking a tongue out - really? TSK!) and didn't fit the characters. <br><br>Also, their names! Their. Names. Should. Be. Changed. Into.<br>Slade - <u> Wink 1 </u><br>Smiley - <u> Wink 2 </u><br>Brass - <u> Wink 3 </u><br>Moon - <u> Wink 4 </u><br>Harley - <u> Wink 5 </u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453292761i/17807733._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453292762i/17807734._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453292762i/17807735._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453292762i/17807736._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b> Wink wink wink wink wink wink wink wink wink wink wink wink wink wink wink. More wink wink wink wink wink. And one more WINK. </b><br><br>Gah! Stop already! No sh*t I was desensitized through and through.<br><br>To be honest, a lot of scenes made my eyes rolled but there's something in this series that makes me wanting to reach for the next sequel. <br>I do hope Valiant won't disappoint.<br><br>Rating it <b>2.5</b> <i>I-dislike-wankers-err-winkers</i> <b>Stars</b><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br>Buddy reading this bad boy with lovely gal pal <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26653561-alp" rel="nofollow noopener">Alp</a> tomorrow, 14th Jan.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3730117985313609557" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--"><img alt="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555353893p2/3161105.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1214648241?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--">Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1214648241" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12092765919914141092"><br/><b>RATING: 1.5-2 Just Meh Hearts. </b><br/><br/>Well, the rating kind of speaks for itself. I really enjoyed the first one in this series, and for all the right reasons too. <i>Slade</i>, in comparison, did not gain any brownie points from me. I'll make this simple, since this entire series is a guilty-pleasure venture for me.<br/><br/><u>What I Liked:</u><br/><br/>1) Dr. Trisha Norbit. It seems the women in this series are just plain old awesome, and full of snark and <i>
  <b>backbone</b>
</i>. No clueless, dumb, or naive women in here, and lets just say, t</span>
  <span id="freeText12092765919914141092" style="display:none"><br /><b>RATING: 1.5-2 Just Meh Hearts. </b><br /><br />Well, the rating kind of speaks for itself. I really enjoyed the first one in this series, and for all the right reasons too. <i>Slade</i>, in comparison, did not gain any brownie points from me. I'll make this simple, since this entire series is a guilty-pleasure venture for me.<br /><br /><u>What I Liked:</u><br /><br />1) Dr. Trisha Norbit. It seems the women in this series are just plain old awesome, and full of snark and <i>
  <b>backbone</b>
</i>. No clueless, dumb, or naive women in here, and lets just say, that goes a long way in making me one happy reader. So, for putting up with Slade's stupidness and for her great personality, Trisha gets a full star. <br /><br />2) The concept. Again, I can't help but be drawn to the concept of this series. The animal/human fusion is interesting, and different. I'm always craving different, so this is my wish come true. Applause for that Laurann Dohner. And I have no doubt, this aspect of the series will keep getting better and better. Hopefully. :P<br /><br />3) Secondary characters. There are so many potential new men being introduced and I am beyond excited for some of there stories, especially Brass, Justice, Tiger, Moon, Harley and Smiley's. They are such a great, humorous bunch, and I can't wait for them to find their own mates. <br /><br />And, that's about where all the good ends, unfortunately.<br /><br /><u>What I didn't Like:</u><br /><br />1) Slade. This guy I could not warm up to. He's an asshole in the worst way possible. He thinks he's funny (you are not, I assure you!), and he is just annoying. Did I mention he is rude? Well he is. I did not like his character, and the way he treated Trisha for most of the book, didn't sit well with me. He left her, and then when something major happens, he was beyond rude to her, blamed her without even asking questions. Idiot. Then all of a sudden at the end he loves her and wants her after everything clears up. Umm...how about no? There was nothing redeemable about him. I was angry at Trisha for taking him back...but...a story's gotta have its HEA, right?<br /><br />2) The ending. Wait...what ending?? There is none. A sudden clearing up of a situation, and cliff drop. The book just ends. I actually was not expecting that. Simply, it was just a bad "ending", there was no lead up to it. I can't describe it any better way than that. Not my thing.<br /><br />3) The plot. I actually did not like the storyline in this. Its so generic and it kind of felt pointless, in my opinion. Majority of the book is Trisha and Slade being on the run from the bad guys in the freakin woods until they can be rescued?? Are you kidding me? You'd think a big, strong beast-man could out run humans, but apparently not. *eye-rolls* By the time it actually kind of got interesting and worth reading, I was past the point of being generous. <br /><br />Overall, not my favourite of the series, but I am hoping <u>Valiant</u> will redeem itself.<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Posted: March 1, 2015</i>
</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2735719430118747618">Way too silly at times. I had to DNF this one because I did a lot of eye-rolling while reading it. SUV tumbles down a ravine, hero & heroine are on the run from the bad guys trying to kill them but hey, let's stop and have some sexytimes even though said guys are still looking for us. If that's not bad enough, heroine is captured by bad guys the next day, is almost raped by one of them and hero saves her at the last minute and THEN, after she has a crying fest about the would be rape, she's want</span>
  <span id="freeText2735719430118747618" style="display:none">Way too silly at times. I had to DNF this one because I did a lot of eye-rolling while reading it. SUV tumbles down a ravine, hero &amp; heroine are on the run from the bad guys trying to kill them but hey, let's stop and have some sexytimes even though said guys are still looking for us. If that's not bad enough, heroine is captured by bad guys the next day, is almost raped by one of them and hero saves her at the last minute and THEN, after she has a crying fest about the would be rape, she's wants to have sex with hero immediately after that scene. Color me confused. They went tumbling down a ravine, in an SUV, where neither was wearing a seatbelt, heroine actually ended up landing in the back of the truck when all was said and done and yet neither is injured to the point where sexytimes was the last thing on their mind? I couldn't keep going with this.</span>

<div id="review_203490448" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/203490448" />
    <a title="Laurie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2241124-laurie"><img alt="Laurie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1364156144p2/2241124.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/203490448?book_show_action=true">Aug 29, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laurie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laurie" href="/user/show/2241124-laurie">Laurie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer203490448" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3127925601519769194">This book is # 2 in Laurann’s new series. Where book # 1 has a more serious feel because it’s setting up the world that the New Species live in. This one has more moments of humor.<br/><br/>Trisha Norbert is an ER doctor. There’s an emergency in her ER. That’s when she meets Slade, who is a New Species. New Species are men made from humans spliced with animal DNA. He is a canine breed, who ends up on Trisha's exam table wounded when he’s rescued from the lab that created him. She can’t forget him and she </span>
  <span id="freeText3127925601519769194" style="display:none">This book is # 2 in Laurann’s new series. Where book # 1 has a more serious feel because it’s setting up the world that the New Species live in. This one has more moments of humor.<br /><br />Trisha Norbert is an ER doctor. There’s an emergency in her ER. That’s when she meets Slade, who is a New Species. New Species are men made from humans spliced with animal DNA. He is a canine breed, who ends up on Trisha's exam table wounded when he’s rescued from the lab that created him. She can’t forget him and she applies to be a doctor at Homeland, the place where the New Species live. When she gets there she meets Slade again but Slade doesn't recognize her. And that’s how their story begins.<br /><br />As characters, Trisha is a smart, sometimes funny woman, but at times seems a bit timid. But she’s brave when she needs to be. Slade is at time arrogant, powerful, has a sense of humor and is loyal but he can be a bit of a jerk. He also shows that he can be vulnerable. As you learn more about his background, you understand the reasons for his behavior! His character is very complex and well rounded. Harley, Brass and Moon are wonderful secondary characters, who I hope get their own books.<br /> <br />This was another great story from Laurann. I start one of her books and can never put it down till it’s finished. Now I just have to wait for the next book in this series which I believe will be Valiant’s story, who you meet in this book.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3127925601519769194" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15198861936178392221">I liked this one.<br/><br/>Ok, so I guess I got pretty lucky with the last few books I've read. And I'm so glad about that! Although well... I am kind of waiting for the other shoe to drop.<br/><br/>Anyway, this book was pretty nice. I liked the characters and I'm glad I got to see a bit what happened with the "New Species" once it escaped the lab.   <span id="freeText15198861936178392221" style="display:none">I liked this one.<br /><br />Ok, so I guess I got pretty lucky with the last few books I've read. And I'm so glad about that! Although well... I am kind of waiting for the other shoe to drop.<br /><br />Anyway, this book was pretty nice. I liked the characters and I'm glad I got to see a bit what happened with the "New Species" once it escaped the lab. Again, I'd have loved a bit more plot, a bit more world-builder, but it was pretty nice. True, not as nice as the previous one, but still, it was good.<br /><br />So, if you liked the other one, you'll probably like this one too. If not... well, try other stuff, there are things you'll like out there!</span>

Now he has to find a way to win her back. <br /><br />Y’all I can’t even tell you how many twists, turns, and completely shocking details this book holds. It has to much to put into words. <span id="freeTextContainer14417222056129147912"><b>ETA: 6/19/18</b><br/><i>Upon reading this one for the second time 6 years later, I had to update my thoughts on Slade & Trisha. What I thought was lacking with them the very first time I read this book, was actually there for me the second time around. I honestly don't know what distracted me from their chemistry the first time; but it was definitely white hot for me now..<br/><br/>I think maybe Slade's attitude is what killed it for me the first time, but reading him again now, I see and understand him better. His m</i></span>
  <span id="freeText14417222056129147912" style="display:none"><b>ETA: 6/19/18</b><br /><i>Upon reading this one for the second time 6 years later, I had to update my thoughts on Slade &amp; Trisha. What I thought was lacking with them the very first time I read this book, was actually there for me the second time around. I honestly don't know what distracted me from their chemistry the first time; but it was definitely white hot for me now..<br /><br />I think maybe Slade's attitude is what killed it for me the first time, but reading him again now, I see and understand him better. His motives. So what I've come to understand about his personality now, didn't take away from them collectively as a couple for me upon this second read. If that makes sense? <br /><br />So I had to add another star to this one and update my thoughts.<br />I really loved this one all around this time :)....... </i><br /><br /><br />The action in this one definitely dominates more so than in the 1st installment. It's alot more suspenseful so it takes on a much more dramatic &amp; serious tone. So I do love that about this one.<br /><br /> But Slade &amp; Trisha, while cute together, didn't exude that passion, that heat, the unyielding emotion that I got from Fury &amp; his mate in the 1st book. And that is what I think I missed the most in this book.<br /><br /> You will love Brass, he's such a sweetheart &amp; I felt really really bad for him in a certain scene. And you meet alot of new &amp; different intriguing New Species, which is great... And I got a GREAT surprise with this story that I did not see coming. I wondered if it would go there, but I still did not see it happening this soon. So it was a nice surprise.<br /><br />Once the emminent danger seems to calm a bit, we get a bit more of the lighter, campy interactions between the characters that was very present in the 1st book. So again, I had alot of laugh out loud sweet endearing moments with this story.<br /><br />I like this 2nd installment and would recommend this read. <br />On to book 3!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2051563155347104263">I'd argue that this is another winner in the series. Were there things about the story that bothered me a bit? Sure. But overall, there is a great story here.<br/><br/>Laurann Dohner has got a great concept. A new species trying to set up in the world rifling with hate-group-hicks just waiting to inject a little bit of suspense into her stories along with the 'we love animal-men' romance that is bound to happen. It's a guaranteed page turner.<br/><br/>I do find the romance side a bit...stiff. I am thinking this mig</span>
  <span id="freeText2051563155347104263" style="display:none">I'd argue that this is another winner in the series. Were there things about the story that bothered me a bit? Sure. But overall, there is a great story here.<br /><br />Laurann Dohner has got a great concept. A new species trying to set up in the world rifling with hate-group-hicks just waiting to inject a little bit of suspense into her stories along with the 'we love animal-men' romance that is bound to happen. It's a guaranteed page turner.<br /><br />I do find the romance side a bit...stiff. I am thinking this might get better as the series (and it looks like it will be a big series) continues because it feels like the kinks about the differences between the new species and humans in the romance department aren't fully worked out. Some developments in the story seem forced or the resolution feels wrong in some way (not totally wrong but it just doesn't sit well). I noticed it in book one and I noticed it here. In this story the emotional relationship between the H/h wasn't exactly fulfilling although the potential was there.<br /><br />That being said, I really liked towards the very end (crisis over) part of the book where the heroine learns that the hero is a slob when she moves in with him. Like a disgustingly messy dude. I really liked reading about developments in how the characters get to know each other even after the bulk of the romance was declared. It's nice to see the relationship constantly evolving as part of the HEA, that doesn't have to do with re-declaring ones love, if you know what I mean.<br /><br />This is a recommended read. If nothing else, the concept is interesting. I can't wait for book #3.<br /></span>

Thankfully I am rereading them again or most of them anyway.<br/><br/>So obviously I wrote that this one wasn't as good as the first one,huh. I lied this one is just as good as the first one if not better. 5 "sweet thing and lollypop" Stars.<br/><br/>We met Trisha in the first book as she started working for NSO. Trisha and Slade have a rocky start. In the second book we see that they met once before and that Slade doesn't recognise D</span>
  <span id="freeText17230501355615443728" style="display:none">First read: 30th April 2013. Might I add that the first review I wrote was awful. Thankfully I am rereading them again or most of them anyway.<br /><br />So obviously I wrote that this one wasn't as good as the first one,huh. I lied this one is just as good as the first one if not better. 5 "sweet thing and lollypop" Stars.<br /><br />We met Trisha in the first book as she started working for NSO. Trisha and Slade have a rocky start. In the second book we see that they met once before and that Slade doesn't recognise Doc, which Trisha is really upset about. The first time around I didn't really connect with Slade but that has changed. Although he is rude and crude he has a lot of charm as well. <br /><br />As a character Trisha is smart, witty and awesome. The banter between Blade and her was epic. <br /><br />Slade snorted. “Women.” “Men.” “Smartass.” “Dumbass.”<br /><br />The plot once again was really good. I like the fact that it took place outside of Homeland. There is a surprise twist to the story but I really don't want to give it away. That there are hate groups and that the real fact is that the humans are the monsters and not NSO. <br /><br />I loved how Moo, Brass and Harley were with one another. So easy going it was a pleasure to read. I have to say though that although the main characters were Slade and Trisha. Valiant is my favourite.<br /><br />Valliant was my favourite. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17230501355615443728" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2700907639" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4433523495304683590"><b>He couldn’t put her in that much danger or ruin her life. She meant too much to him.</b> <br/><br/>I’m in the minority here where I find Slade to be selfless and extremely caring. Leaving Trisha almost killed him but he honestly thought it would be best for her. Was it? Of course not. Jeez. He could have asked her what she wanted to do. But of course the book would have been over so the miscommunication must continue. The only complain I have is that it wasn’t emotional enough for me. I feel like it was a hug</span>
  <span id="freeText4433523495304683590" style="display:none"><b>He couldn’t put her in that much danger or ruin her life. She meant too much to him.</b> <br /><br />I’m in the minority here where I find Slade to be selfless and extremely caring. Leaving Trisha almost killed him but he honestly thought it would be best for her. Was it? Of course not. Jeez. He could have asked her what she wanted to do. But of course the book would have been over so the miscommunication must continue. The only complain I have is that it wasn’t emotional enough for me. I feel like it was a huge missed opportunity. There was so much to work with. I remember crying in book one. I didn’t cry at all reading this one. Maybe the funny guys helped. Even though I didn’t really like their jokes. 🤷🏻‍♀️ Again, minority here. <br /><br />That ending was so abrupt too. I thought there was a glitch on my ebook. Lol. But that just means I need to start book 3 ASAP. Which, gah!!!! Valiant!! I can’t wait to read about the lion man. Even though I want Justice’s story now. I’m willing to wait if I get lion man. I am wondering if some of the really savage New Species have antlers though. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('E/QX3gGjtCsmyjoDIFpzcnYXyjYiHSs9xpTpcq7WARzPQOQHYpxBF1PJJx3zWRHZxiIh+yhq1LcxYGtrRzVvIA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('F4GsgJ2D057kHUItKZ5aqLvTqUJj0g6AuMVgjNM07J/LNV9Z/rwmopEeXzP6nTgDC+ZCj2ml8QpPMeKVOteCow==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3185926387031838986">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've alw</span>
  <span id="freeText3185926387031838986" style="display:none">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've always been a daydreamer, and I'm a HUGE fan of books, always have been.<br /><br />No, I didn't know that I always wanted to write. I inhaled books as a child. I read entire series (Pippi Longstocking, Nancy Drew and The Hardy Boys, Trixie Beldon, The Borrowers, etc) in a matter of days at a time. By the time I was nine years old I had an adult library card where I visited often. I moved on to John Saul, Stephen King, Richard Laymon, Agatha Christie, and then found romance. I was hooked. I wrote poetry in my teens and then moved on to short stories. My first book was started after I read a real bomb of a book that ticked me off with really horrible characters and a plot that was shabby at best and I thought... I could do better. LOL.<br /><br />I wrote my first book which will probably never see the light of day in the early 90's. I wrote a series of a few books from it. I'm a series fan! I kept writing for fun, wrote MANY books and then in 2009 I decided to try to get published. I wrote my first Sci Fi romance and Ral's Woman came to be. I submitted it and with a little tweaking, Ellorascave sent me an acceptance letter. It was kind of a 'Cinderella' experience for me. It's been a terrific ride so far and I'm really happy that I finally had the time to commit to writing full time. It's a dream come true.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3185926387031838986" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>

        $('bookCover_16005363').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
